<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:полемический.html>полеми́ческий</a> (27079)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">polém(ique)</i> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ческий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-íčeskij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полемический.html>полеми́ческий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">polemíčeskij</span>) (<i>no comparative</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>polemical</li>
<li>fervent, passionate</li></ol>

***полениться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:полениться.html>полени́ться</a> (13048)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-лени́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-lenítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, or directly from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лениться.html>лени́ться</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lenítʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полениться.html>полени́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">polenítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to be lazy
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:полениться.html>полени́лся</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:позвонить.html>позвони́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>мне</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on ne <b>polenílsja</b> pozvonítʹ mne</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he gave himself the trouble to call me</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лениться.html>лени́ться</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">lenítʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лень.html>лень</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">lenʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:леность.html>ле́ность</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">lénostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ленивый.html>лени́вый</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">lenívyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">лени́вец</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">lenívec</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***полено.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:полено.html>полено</a> (8691)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">полѣно</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">polěno</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, related to <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">полѣти</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">polěti</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">burn, flame</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полено.html>поле́но</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poléno</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полено.html>поле́на</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полено.html>поле́нья</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полено.html>поле́ньев</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>billet, log, chock (of wood), wood block <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">for use as firewood</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>log-shaped cake, e.g. a Yule log</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:полетать.html>полета́ть</a> (28258)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:летать.html>лета́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">letátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полетать.html>полета́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poletátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:летать.html>лета́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to fly</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:летать.html>лета́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">letátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полетать.html>полета́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">poletátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, are abstract verbs. Their counterparts, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лететь.html>лете́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">letétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полететь.html>полете́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">poletétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> are Russian concrete verbs.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:полететь.html>полете́ть</a> (2625)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лететь.html>лете́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">letétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полететь.html>полете́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poletétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лететь.html>лете́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to fly, to be flying</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лететь.html>лете́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">letétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полететь.html>полете́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">poletétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> are Russian concrete verbs. Their counterparts, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:летать.html>лета́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">letátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полетать.html>полета́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">poletátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, are abstract verbs.
</p>

***полечь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:полечь.html>поле́чь</a> (21067)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лечь.html>лечь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lečʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полечь.html>поле́чь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poléčʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">полега́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">perfective only</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to die or be killed in battle <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of all or many people</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">perfective only<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to lie down <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of all or many people</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to bend to the ground <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of cereal grains or trees</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">полега́емость</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">polegájemostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***ползать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ползать.html>по́лзать</a> (5171)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*pь̀lzati</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ползать.html>по́лзать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pólzatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">попо́лзать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to creep, to crawl</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ползать.html>По́лзать</a></b> is a Russian abstract verb. Its unidirectional counterparts, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ползти.html>ползти́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">polztí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поползти.html>поползти́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">popolztí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> are concrete verbs.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><i>See <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ползти.html>ползти́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">polztí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> for derived verbs.</i></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">ползание</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">polzanije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поползновение.html>поползнове́ние</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">popolznovénije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">поползень</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">popolzenʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">о́ползень</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ópolzenʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">ползунки</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">polzunki</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***ползти.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ползти.html>ползти́</a> (2365)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ползти.html>ползти́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">polztí</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поползти.html>поползти́</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to creep, to crawl</li>
<li>to move slowly</li>
<li>to spread <i>(of rumours)</i></li>
<li>to fray, to ravel out <i>(of fabric)</i></li>
<li>to slip, to collapse <i>(of soil)</i></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ползти.html>ползти́</a></b> and <b><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поползти.html>поползти́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">popolztí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></b> are Russian concrete verbs. Their counterpart, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ползать.html>по́лзать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pólzatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, is an abstract verb.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<div class="derivedterms" style="column-count: 2; -moz-column-count: 2; -ms-column-count: 2; -o-column-count: 2; -webkit-column-count: 2;;">

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">всполза́ть</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vspolzátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выползать.html>выполза́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vypolzátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">дополза́ть</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">dopolzátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<li>(no equivalent)</li>
<li>(no equivalent)</li>
<li>(no equivalent)</li>

<p><a href = vnd.unilang:общий.html>О́бщее</a> прототипическое <a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>значе́ние</a> — <i><a href = vnd.unilang:медленно.html>ме́дленно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:двигаться.html>дви́гаться</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:определенный.html>определённом</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:направление.html>направле́нии</a></i>.
</p>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ползти.html>ползти́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">polztí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-у́чий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-účij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<ol><li>crawling, creeping

<li>creeping
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ползучий.html>ползу́чая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:инфляция.html>инфля́ция</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>polzúčaja</b> infljácija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">creeping inflation</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ползти.html>ползу́щий</a> (2365)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***полировать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:полировать.html>полирова́ть</a> (8679)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">polieren</i>, which is borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">polir</i> (see modern French <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">polir</i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">polīre</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to polish</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полировать.html>полирова́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">polirovátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отполировать.html>отполирова́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to polish, to shine, to buff</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полировка.html>полиро́вка</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">poliróvka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">полировочный</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">polirovočnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">политура</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">politura</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***полиставший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:полиставший.html>полиста́вший</a> (12667)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полиставший.html>полиста́вший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">polistávšij</span>)

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:политика.html>поли́тика</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">polítika</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:политика.html>поли́тики</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:политика.html>поли́тики</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:политика.html>поли́тик</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>politics
<dl><dd><dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">“Я <a href = vnd.unilang:прийти.html>пришёл</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вывод.html>вы́воду</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:политика.html>поли́тика</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:слишком.html>сли́шком</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:серьезный.html>серьёзное</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:занятие.html>заня́тие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:чтобы.html>что́бы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>её</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:доверять.html>доверя́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:политика.html>поли́тикам</a>.” <i>― Шарль <a href = vnd.unilang:де.html>де</a> Голль</i></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">“Ja prišól k vývodu što <b>polítika</b> éto slíškom serʹjóznoje zanjátije štóby jejó doverjátʹ polítikam.” <i>― Šarlʹ de Gollʹ</i></i> ― <span class="e-translation"><br />“I have come to the conclusion that politics is too serious a matter to be left to the politicians.” <i>― Charles de Gaulle</i></span></div></dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li>policy
